The following information refers to symbols present in Geoffrey Pullum and William Ladusaw, _Phonetic Symbol Guide_, 2nd edn (Chicago: The University of Chicago Press, 1996).

#### Unicode characters

The following table shows the Unicode characters that have equivalent symbols given in _Phonetic Symbol Guide_.

Note 1: It is preferable to use precomposed characters with the tilde and hooks as found in the Phonetic Extensions block or IPA Extensions block.

Note 2: Use 01E5 unless the 0067 vs 0261 distinction should be kept for barred/crossed forms.

Note 3: Use 0038 unless a case pair distinction is required. In the case of Algonquin, Huron use [0222](/char/U000222) and [0223](/char/U000223).

#### Unicode character sequences

The following symbols correspond to a sequence of Unicode characters.

| ID | Name | Graphics | USVs | Comment |
| --- | ---- | -------- | ---- | ------- |
| PSG2.010.1 | Overdot Turned Script A | :usv[0252]{char}:usv[0307]{char} | [0252](/char/U000252) [0307](/char/U000307) |  |
